The Shanghai-Changzhou Commuter Train Caused an Accident Yesterday Afternoon When It Arrived at the North Station Due to Overly Aggressive Braking Upon Entering the Station, Four Wheels Jumped Off the Track, Destroying One Third-Class Passenger Car and Several Sections of the Platform Roof. The Loss Is Estimated at More Than 10,000 Yuan

Seven People Including the Conductor, Passengers, and Railway Police Were Injured

The 17th Changzhou-Shanghai commuter train on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway caused the complete destruction of the last third-class baggage and passenger car, IBV No. 943, and the partial destruction of the third-class passenger car TP758 at 11:32 AM yesterday when it arrived at the North Station Yangqi section. The fourth track, the 26th turnout, and platforms 5 and 6 and their roofs were also damaged. The conductor, Li Shijun, as well as three passengers, two railway police officers, and one employee of the Datong Transportation Company were injured at the scene and have been admitted to the Railway Hospital for treatment. The details are recorded as follows:

Circumstances of the Accident

The 17th Changzhou-Shanghai commuter train on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway departed from Changzhou at 6:00 AM yesterday. According to the timetable, it was supposed to arrive in Shanghai at 11:35 AM, but it traveled faster than expected yesterday and arrived three minutes early. When the train reached the North Yangqi section on the Hanqiao Bridge, it should have entered the fifth track and stopped at platform 6. Unexpectedly, the frog of the turnout there was not tightly connected and was loosened after the vibration. When the last (TBV) third-class and baggage mixed car No. 943 passed over it, the rear four wheels of the car turned into the fourth track due to the change in the direction of the frog. However, the fourth and fifth tracks were separated by a platform. As the front and rear wheels of the car traveled in different directions, the car body crossed the platform and advanced, first breaking the cement pillars of the two platforms, and the roof also collapsed immediately, destroying more than two zhang (approximately 6.6 meters). The sound was as loud as the explosion of a giant bomb. For a time, the passengers on the train were all frightened and at a loss. Before long, the front and rear wheels all fell off and sank on the fourth and fifth tracks, respectively. However, the car did not stop at this time, so the car body was dragged off the platform and onto the fifth track. After being shaken again, the middle of the car body was broken and fell on the left side of platform 6.

Seven People Injured

The injured in the train derailment included the guard Li Shijun, three passengers (two men and one woman), two railway police officers, and one silver dollar escort from the Dafeng Company, totaling seven people. Except for the heavily injured Dafeng Company escort who was sent to Renji Hospital, the rest were sent to the Railway Hospital by train.

Overview of the Damage

The damage included the complete destruction of one TBV 943 baggage and third-class passenger mixed car, the rear end of the TP756 third-class passenger car, and partial damage to the PC3 flower car. More than ten zhang of platform 6, more than ten zhang of platform 5, the frogs of the fourth and fifth tracks, two cement pillars of the platform roof, more than three zhang of the roof, more than two zhang of track, and twenty-seven sleepers were destroyed. The estimated material loss is about more than 10,000 yuan.

Police Dispatched to Maintain Order

After the incident, Director Xiao of the Transportation Department, Deputy Director Liu, and the stationmaster rushed to the scene to inspect. They first sent the injured to the hospital for treatment and informed Director Huang Boqiao by telegram. They also notified the Mechanical and Engineering Departments to send workers to repair the damage and dispatched a large number of railway police to stand at the entrances of platforms 5 and 6 and the scene of the accident, strictly prohibiting outsiders from entering to observe.

Actively Repairing

After the incident, the Transportation Department immediately notified the Wusong Machine Factory and the Engineering and Mechanical Departments by telephone, dispatching a large number of workers to actively repair the damage. Upon receiving the telegram, the Wusong Machine Factory immediately dispatched two rescue vehicles, carrying 246 workers, and a crane to the scene of the accident. They first lifted the derailed passenger car onto the rescue vehicle with the crane and drove to the Wusong Machine Factory for repairs. They also dismantled the roof and replaced the track sleepers. All repairs were completed by 7:00 PM.

Investigating the Cause of the Accident

Director Huang Boqiao of the Two-Road Administration went to the scene to investigate at 2:00 PM yesterday, considering the bizarre nature of the incident and the responsibility for it urgently needed to be investigated. He immediately summoned the Director and Deputy Director of the Transportation Department, the Director and Deputy Director of the Engineering Department, the Director and Deputy Director of the Mechanical Department, the driver of the derailed train, the stationmaster of the North Station, the Chief Inspector, and the Chief of the General Section to hold a temporary emergency meeting in the North Station conference room to discuss the cause of the accident. The meeting adjourned at 4:00 PM. The results of the meeting have not yet been released.

The City Finance Bureau Prepares to Take Over the Business License Tax for Tobacco and Alcohol, Which Will Be Entirely Transferred to Local Governments Starting from July 1

Regarding the case of transferring the business license tax for tobacco and alcohol to the provinces and cities for collection, after the city government approved the request from the Ministry of Finance to investigate and handle the matter, the city government specifically ordered the city finance bureau yesterday to prepare to take over the collection within a specified period, starting from July 1. The original order of the city government is recorded as follows: According to the Ministry of Finance's inquiry, the business license tax for tobacco and alcohol is essentially a business tax. In June of the 20th year of the Republic of China, the National Government promulgated the Business Tax Law, which stipulated in Article 2 that "the central government shall collect the business license tax for tobacco and alcohol. After retaining one-tenth for the central government, the rest should be allocated to the provinces and cities as local revenue." The stamp tax and tobacco and alcohol tax bureaus of the provinces under the jurisdiction of the Ministry have been collecting and allocating funds in accordance with regulations. After the abolition of miscellaneous taxes and fees, the method of compensation was determined by the conference resolution to transfer all business license tax for tobacco and alcohol to local governments for collection in order to increase revenue, considering the possibility of insufficient local financial resources. The secretariat of the conference presented the resolution for review and handling. The Ministry re-examined and verified that this business license tax for tobacco and alcohol should be collected by the central government according to the provisions of the Business Tax Law. However, given the aforementioned situation, the Ministry should approve the change to local self-management in order to adjust local finances and facilitate collection. It is now scheduled to be implemented from July 1 of this year. Please instruct your city government to instruct the finance bureau to follow the central laws and regulations to collect the tax. The Ministry will still print the required licenses for whole or retail sales of tobacco and alcohol in spring, summer, autumn, and winter, and instruct the bureau to list the detailed numbers, prepare the printing costs, and present them to the Ministry for collection in order to unify and facilitate verification. The detailed rules for implementation are attached, and please instruct your city government to investigate and handle them, and report the handling situation after the takeover and how to reduce the burden on the people at any time for verification. The provisional regulations for the business license tax for tobacco and alcohol and the detailed rules for implementation are attached. This order is hereby issued to the bureau for compliance (the regulations are omitted).

The City Farmers' Association Submits a Request to the Social Affairs Bureau to Stop the Rise in Rice Prices, as It Does Not Benefit Farmers and Instead Increases Their Burden, and Should Be Stopped to Avoid Affecting People's Food Supply

This summer has been rainless and the weather is extremely hot. It is generally speculated that a drought has formed. Rice merchants are taking the opportunity to raise rice prices. The Farmers' Association believes that the rise in rice prices not only affects people's food supply but also has a great impact on the livelihood of farmers. Yesterday, it specially submitted a request to the Social Affairs Bureau to stop the continued rise in rice prices in order to maintain the livelihood of farmers and benefit people's food supply. The original request is recorded as follows: For the soaring rice prices, profiteers monopolize and hoard, please devise a way to stop them, to maintain the livelihood of farmers and benefit the people's food affairs. I have learned that this summer, the seasonal rains have been out of order, and the weather is dry. The ports and rivers are dry. The farmland in the four rural villages lacks rain. As a result, rice and cotton crops are both lacking rain and are scorched by the scorching sun, showing a withered and poor harvest. Farmers are worried and worried. At this time of drought and disaster, and at the time of the green and yellow shortages, rice prices have suddenly risen and are continuing to rise daily. The future of the people's food supply is greatly affected, and the impact on farmers is particularly significant. In recent years, rural areas have gone bankrupt, and the farmers' economy has become increasingly impoverished. The income from the harvest is not enough to provide warmth and fullness for a family. How can there be surplus grain for profit? The rise in rice prices, according to the saying that cheap grain hurts farmers, must think that this can increase the income of farmers, but do not know that in fact, it is no different from increasing the hardship of farmers' livelihoods. Because farmers often eat next year's food this year, and the income from the harvest is not enough to repay debts, let alone anything else. Once the harvest is sold, it is sold out. The current rise in rice prices not only does not help farmers but also increases the burden on farmers, and is only for general profiteers to hoard and monopolize to enrich their own pockets. I believe that people's food supply is the lifeline of the country, and farmers are the source of people's food supply. Looking forward to the future, the hidden worries are endless. Therefore, I dare to prepare a document and ask your bureau to devise a way to stop it, so that each stone (approximately 59.2 kg) does not exceed ten yuan, in order to maintain the livelihood of farmers and benefit the people's food supply. I implore you to be considerate of the people's difficulties and grant what I have requested. I am anxiously awaiting orders, and I present this to Wu, the Director of the Shanghai City Social Affairs Bureau.

After the U.S. dockworkers went on strike, the Seattle route on the Shanghai-Pacific route has been completely blocked, and no ships have come. Those on the San Francisco route have also changed to Los Angeles. The losses suffered by the shipping companies in Shanghai are very large, especially the U.S. Mail Company. From May 18 to the present, the Seattle route alone has been stopped due to the strike, and the number of passengers who were unable to depart and therefore refunded their tickets is no less than a thousand, including group passengers, in Shanghai, Hong Kong, and Xiaoluson. Some have changed to take ships to Vancouver and Los Angeles. Also, after the strike, the number of mail ships in the Pacific has been greatly reduced, and many ships have been stationed in various ports. Yesterday, the local Dalai Foreign Firm received a telegram from its head office that the four mail ships blocked in Seattle, including the President Grant, have found a way to unload the accumulated cargo from the ship, and the ship can resume sailing from Seattle today. The other ships, such as the President McKinley, the President Jackson, and the President Jefferson, are also finding ways to restore the Sino-U.S. route.

The Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation Changes the Call Method in Each District, Expands the Number of Lines Connecting to the Concession to Seventy Pairs, and Specifies Three Types of Small Private Branch Exchanges

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, the new phone book of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation changes the call method. The details are recorded as follows:

Call Method in Each District The new phone book of the Telephone Bureau specifies the call method in each district: (A) For calls from Nanshi, Zhabei, and Longhua to various districts, (1) The mutual call method is still the same as the automatic telephone method, dialing directly; (2) To connect to Pudong, dial 36; to Jiangwan, dial 41161; to Zhenru (attached to Nanxiang), dial 41141; to Wusong (attached to Baoshan), dial 41181; (3) To connect to the concession, listen for the "0" sound and transfer the number; (B) For calls from Pudong, Jiangwan, Zhenru, and Wusong to various districts, (1) The mutual call method is to call according to the shared telephone method; (2) To connect to Nanshi, Zhabei, and Longhua, listen for the call according to the magneto telephone method; (3) To connect to the concession, listen for the call according to the magneto telephone method. The new phone book has been printed and distributed to users.

Increasing the Number of Lines Connecting to the Concession In order to maintain convenient communication, the bureau has changed the lines connecting Nanshi to the concession to underground lines, and the lines in Zhabei to armored cables. In addition to the completion of the Nanshi part, the telephone branch bureau in the city center will be established in August since its construction. In addition, due to the busy communication between the Chinese concession and the rental concession, the bureau has decided to expand the "0" switchboard starting next month, increasing it from fifty pairs of lines to seventy pairs, in order to facilitate user communication.

Small Private Branch Exchange Styles The bureau also believes that the small private branch exchanges of users in various districts have different styles and are difficult to maintain. Therefore, it has been approved by the Ministry of Transportation to divide them into three types according to the needs of users: mutual communication type, board key type, and standing type, depending on the number of relay lines and extensions. Those with one to ten extensions use the board key type, and those with sixteen to fifty extensions use the standing type. The Chief Engineer of the Bureau, Yu Bingjian, has been conducting inspections in various districts for this purpose in recent days in order to proceed with the project.

The Lawyers' Association Requests Again to Abolish the Real Estate Mortgage Rules, as They Conflict with the Civil Code

The Shanghai Lawyers' Association, in opposition to the Shanghai City Government's approval and promulgation of the Real Estate Mortgage Registration Rules by the Land Bureau, believes that the city's individual rules clearly conflict with the current Civil Code. It has petitioned the Ministry of Judicial Administration to forward it to the Executive Yuan, requesting that the Shanghai City Government be ordered to abolish these city's individual rules. After the approval of the Yuan and Ministry, it was not approved and has been delayed until now. Recently, a member, Qian Zhongdao, made a suggestion, requesting that the association continue to petition the Yuan and Ministry, ordering the abolition to correct the situation. After the association submitted it to the joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committee members, the meeting decided to pass it. It immediately appointed a drafting committee to draft a document to petition the Ministry of Judicial Administration and specially submit it to the Executive Yuan for continued petition. It has been issued yesterday, and the original text roughly states that the city's individual rules do conflict with the current Civil Code. Please forward it to the Executive Yuan to order the Shanghai City Government to immediately abolish the Real Estate Mortgage Registration Rules approved and promulgated by the Land Bureau in order to correct the situation. It is really a public envoy. (The original text is omitted)

Wang Xiaolai Resigns as Supervisor of the City Chamber of Commerce

Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce, has presided over the affairs of the association for four years and was re-elected as a supervisor in this election. Mr. Wang has been serving merchant organizations for fifteen years and is exhausted physically and mentally and urgently needs to rest. He sent a special letter of resignation yesterday, stating in the letter: I am writing to inform you that the Chamber of Commerce Law stipulates that the term of office of executive and supervisory committee members is four years and cannot be re-elected. The intention of the legislation is to average work and rest on the one hand, and to prevent control on the other hand. If an executive committee member completes his term of office and is still a supervisor, although the duties of the association are different, he cannot shirk his responsibility. Moreover, if an executive committee member completes his term of office and is elected as a supervisor, and a supervisor completes his term of office and is again elected as an executive committee member, it is different in name but the same in reality. It is a permanent re-election without re-election. Xiaolai believes that this is not possible. From Xiaolai's personal point of view, he has been serving as a member and director of the Chamber of Commerce for fifteen years. Since he served as the Chairman of the Zhabei Chamber of Commerce, the Association for the Business Exhibition, and the Committee for the Reorganization of Merchant Organizations, and until the four-year term of office of the Chairman of the City Chamber of Commerce is over, it has been eight years. The scope of serving the society has been expanding day by day, and the operation of private businesses has been almost completely abandoned. Xiaolai believes that he did not become rich by serving the society, but gradually became thin due to taking care of production. This heart can be seen by heaven and earth. It is also what is called one is happy, one is afraid. What is happy is that in the past terms of office, I did not seek merit, but I was not ashamed. All matters were handled with public tolerance, strictness, and emphasis on honesty. I can be responsible for the two words "honesty". What is afraid is that if this continues, I will lose sight of one thing while paying attention to another. If I do not plan for production, there will be a day when I will break my foot and overturn the pot. How can I be sustained by sacrificing myself to cultivate others? Thinking of this, I shudder. Therefore, I specially express my sincerity and ask to be allowed to resign from the position of supervisor and have the candidate supervisor take over in accordance with the regulations. Xiaolai recalls that during his term of office, in the Zhabei Chamber of Commerce, in the 16th year of the Republic of China, he drove Sun out of the market in order to stabilize Jiangnan. In the City Chamber of Commerce, in the 128th year, he resisted Japan in order to protect the national territory. Although the internal and external troubles are different, the urgency of pacification and supply is the same. I forgot to dress and eat and spent the night without sleep. After a life of worry, I will not cherish it again. In the future, I will still use the qualifications of a member representative to assist at any time, and I will not dare not strive to do what I can. This is to inform you specifically, and I hope you will understand it. This is addressed to the Executive Committee and Supervisory Committee of the Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce. June 29.

The Public Works Department Holds the Licensing of Private Rickshaw Pullers

The Public Works Department announced that starting from July 1 of this year, when a private rickshaw is donated to the Bureau, a notice will be issued, explaining the procedures for the private rickshaw puller to obtain a license. This notice is divided into yellow and blue. Those who receive the yellow form must go to the Xinzha Office (near the Maigen Road Bridge) to apply for a license, and those who receive the blue form must go to the Hongkou Office (corner of Baz Road and Wusong Road) to apply for a license. The owner can freely apply for a yellow or blue notice. The Public Works Department will give as much consideration as possible to whether the distance between the licensee and the office is convenient. The date when the licensing will be implemented will be announced after the Bureau decides.

News of the Labor Strike at the British American Tobacco Factory: Public Security Bureau Orders Union to Withdraw Maintenance Team; City Government Responds, Vowing No Illegal Interference

Yesterday at 1 PM, Zhang Mingqin, the Director of the Public Security Bureau of the Three Districts of Pudong, summoned

Chen Peide and other strike committee members of the British American Tobacco Factory to the bureau for a discussion. He stated that he was under orders from Mayor Wu to demand that the union withdraw the maintenance team stationed near the British American Tobacco Factory by 12 PM tomorrow. Upon hearing this news, all the strike committee members were extremely shocked. They immediately returned to the union, convened an emergency meeting, and collectively went to the City Government to inquire whether Mayor Wu had issued such an order. Since Mayor Wu was not in his office, Zhang Shiwu of the Second Section received them. First, the union representative stated that the purpose of organizing the maintenance team was to ensure the factory's safety and the workers' order, which was beneficial to both labor and management. He emphasized that under no circumstances could they easily withdraw the team before the dispute was resolved. Mr. Zhang replied in person that the City Government would never illegally interfere, and asked them to return. The union representatives then left. The union also stated that the workers were suffering unbearably due to the prolonged strike. They had previously sent a telegram to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek for relief and had now received a reply stating that it had been forwarded to Shanghai Mayor Wu for verification and handling. The union will continue to send representatives to the City Government tomorrow to petition for the prompt allocation of funds for relief to sustain the lives of all workers. It is reported that various support organizations were outraged by the union's report and will also convene an emergency meeting tomorrow morning to express their strong views.

Committee Meeting of the Shanghai County Anti-Smoking Association

The Shanghai County Anti-Smoking Committee held its third meeting yesterday. Four committee members attended, and district chiefs and others were present as observers. The Xinwei Relief Association rented several shikumen houses on Jules Brunat Road in the French Concession in April of last year to accommodate 157 dependents of anti-Japanese general Wang Delin and his troops, providing food, lodging, and medical expenses. It has been over a year since then. Subsequently, free boat and train tickets were issued to 110 people to return to their hometowns. It is now known that the association will end at the end of this month. Therefore, Mr. Li specifically sent a letter to the association yesterday to prepare for the takeover, and continue to rent the house at 25 Jules Brunat Road, "Stating briefly, all applicable furniture is still requested to be allowed to be borrowed by your association, and will be returned in full after the entire family is sent to Xinjiang. Wang Yutong to Visit Japan for Investigation

Economist and international affairs expert Mr. Wang Yutong has recently observed that China's urban industry and commerce have been sluggish in recent years, and the rural economy is declining. The danger of the future is self-evident. Mr. Wang believes that Japan was affected by the aftermath of the global economic downturn a few years ago, especially in rural areas. Therefore, he plans to personally visit Japan to investigate the government and financial sector's relief efforts for rural areas and to travel extensively throughout the country to investigate the general economic situation, hoping to learn from their experience. It is reported that he is scheduled to depart in mid-July and will take a boat to Japan.

Two Fires in the International Settlement

The Yimeng Department Store at No. 373 Mantingfang, West Wuma Road, Mantingfang, caught fire around 1:45 PM yesterday. The flames rose rapidly, breaking through the roof. The upper floor of the building was a warehouse, and sparks immediately flew in, causing significant damage to the imported and general merchandise. The fire brigade rushed to the scene and extinguished the fire around 3 PM. As a result, the entire floor was burned down, and the water damage to the goods was estimated at around 2,000 to 3,000 taels. It is reported that the store had fire insurance.

The Deshengchang Paper Store at No. 110, the corner of Ganzhou Road and Yangzhuo Road, Ganzhou Road, suddenly caught fire at 8:57 PM last night. Thick smoke billowed out, and the fire spread for a long time. It is estimated that two floors were burned down. The fire brigade rushed to the scene and extinguished the fire.

Continuous Hot Weather Causes Drought; Many Narrow Rivers in Rural Areas Gradually Drying Up; Farmers Compete to Draw Water, Fearing Disappointing Autumn Harvest

The weather has been extremely hot recently. According to the astronomical observatory, it is the hottest in sixty years. Currently, although the farmers in the countryside have finished transplanting rice seedlings, they desperately need water. They are drawing water from the rivers, but if it continues to not rain, the rivers will dry up, making it impossible to draw water, and the autumn harvest will be disappointing. Regarding ship traffic, according to people from the countryside, they have to get into the water and push the boats in shallow areas, otherwise they cannot move forward. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency specifically interviewed the Inland Waterways Navigation Bureau yesterday to inquire whether there were any obstacles to ships traveling to the interior. According to the bureau, ships traveling from Shanghai to the interior, such as Pinghu, Suzhou, Wuxi, Huzhou, Changshu, etc., are operating as usual and have not been affected in any way. However, rivers in small towns and cities between urban and rural areas have been affected by farmers drawing water for irrigation and the lack of rain, and most of them are experiencing drought.

Kidnapper Lu Jinbao Executed by Firing Squad; Elderly Father, Sisters, and Brothers Arrive at Court for Final Farewell; Lu Comforts Them and Asks Them Not to Grieve

Lu Jinbao, also known as Yunlun, a kidnapper from Taizhou, was sentenced to death by the First Special District Court and approved by the Jiangsu Provincial Government for kidnapping Sheng Yishao from No. 22 Shandong Road on September 2nd of the previous year and demanding a large ransom. Yesterday morning, the police brought the criminal Lu to the Third Criminal Court, where Judge Shen Shou Zeng asked him if he had any last words or letters for his family. Lu replied that his elderly father, sisters, and brothers were all in court and had brought a package of clothes. He asked the court to allow him to say a few words to his father. He then told his father, "I deserve to die for my crime. Please don't be too upset. Take care of yourself in your old age and don't meddle in other people's affairs in the future." He also told his sisters and brothers not to grieve and to go to the execution ground to collect his body. Judge Shen Shou Zeng ordered Lu Jinbao to be sent to the Shanghai District Procuratorate for execution by firing squad according to the law. Li Zhishan, a lawyer from the Shanghai Municipal Council, took photos and copies of the entire case file. Under the escort of Chinese and foreign police officers, Lu was taken by car to the Caohejing execution ground, where the prosecutor verified Lu's identity and ordered the judicial police to bind him and execute him by firing squad according to the law.

Extortionists Active on Tram No. 18; Demanding 700 Yuan After Several Negotiations; Extortionist Arrested During Payment

Zhang Deming, a native of Ningbo and owner of a transportation company at No. 57 Chengkang Lane, Tangshan Road, received four threatening letters from extortionists between the 21st and 28th of this month, demanding 50,000 yuan, otherwise they would resort to drastic measures to set fire to his house and endanger his son-in-law and others. He was instructed to send a representative or himself to ride Tram No. 18 with a pack of cigarettes as a signal, at Zhaofeng Road, Xujiahui Road, Kangti Road, etc. Someone in the tram would negotiate. Zhang initially ignored the letters, but after receiving more letters with the same content and two bullets as a warning, Shi Jiugen, an employee of Zhang, followed the instructions in the letter, rode the tram to observe the situation, after Xinjihang Road, a man in black clothes, wearing black glasses, holding a wallet with something resembling a pistol inside, asked Shi whether what he wanted was consistent, saying that he could avoid the disaster by giving him several thousand gold. Shi agreed to give him 200 yuan, but he refused because the amount was too small. Later, another letter came, inviting Shi to contact him near the Great World in Tibet Road. Shi went, but he did not arrive. Later, Shi met this person again on the tram at Dongyouheng Road, and they talked again, at least 700 yuan, an appointment was made to make the payment at the Hongkou vegetable market on Gordon Road on the morning of the day before yesterday. Zhang then reported to the Huishan Police Station, which sent Chinese detective Sun Aizhong, accompanied by Shi, with 250 silver dollars wrapped in paper, to wait at the designated location. After a while, a Ningbo native, Chen Ading, staggered to the scene and attempted to take the money from Shi and escape. He was immediately arrested and taken to the police station. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Li Zhishan, a lawyer from the Shanghai Municipal Council, stated that the defendant claimed at the police station that he was a docker and that someone named Jia had asked him to collect the money on his behalf for two yuan. He requested a postponement for further investigation. Judge Xiao ordered him to be detained and the case to be reviewed at a later date.

When the first prize number was drawn, the whole venue burst into an uproar. However, when the number was announced for the last twentieth time as No. 025251, another person announced that the first prize, worth 500,000 yuan, had not been won. The audience checked the lottery tickets they had brought to see if they were lucky enough to win, but the excitement of hoping for several hours suddenly faded, and many people quietly left the venue.

Rickshaw Committee to Hold Meeting to Discuss Licensing Issues

The International Settlement Rickshaw Committee announced yesterday that the monthly fee for each rickshaw substitute donor license is 15 yuan and 67 cents. According to a statement issued by the person in charge of the Rickshaw Industry Office in the Special District, the monthly fee for each rickshaw license in the British Concession is 2 yuan and 4 cents, 2 yuan and 2 cents in the French Concession, and 1 yuan and 5 cents in the Chinese Concession, plus 10 cents for the association fee and 5 cents for the material donation, totaling 5 yuan and 26 cents. Substitute donors pay for licenses, vehicle inspections, and other matters, so they collect a total of 5 yuan and 50 cents per month, with a profit of only 24 cents. However, the Rickshaw Committee announced that according to reports from rickshaw owners, many owners who wanted to obtain licenses themselves were blocked. All kinds of statements are unfounded. The rickshaw merchants resolved at the last rickshaw owners' conference that they were unwilling to accept the Rickshaw Committee's facilities and refused to do so. Therefore, it was not the substitute donors who blocked them. They also requested the Municipal Council to revoke the name of the Rickshaw Committee and return all rickshaw matters to the jurisdiction of the Vehicle Affairs Department. Now, the committee actually claims that the owners agree with the Rickshaw Committee's proposals. Moreover, according to the notices recently distributed by the Rickshaw Committee to various rickshaws, they want to obtain certificates. Therefore, the industry has decided to hold a general meeting at the association at 3 PM tomorrow (30th) to discuss this matter. At the same time, due to the establishment of a clinic and pharmacy, they will make plans for the establishment.

Telegram Bureau Notice: Method for Recording Telegram Receipts

The Shanghai Telegram Bureau of the Ministry of Communications of the National Government recently issued a notice stating: 1. Starting July 1st, all domestic wireless telegraph receipts for accounting purposes will be based on the new telegraph receipt signature books issued by this Bureau. Telegrams will not be accepted from those without the books or those who do not carry them. 2. For customers who have already deposited a telegraph guarantee deposit or have a bank guarantee letter with this Bureau, the Bureau will gradually distribute new telegraph receipt signature books starting June 20th. If any are missed or not received before the end of June, please inquire with the Bureau. 3. The signature books for military and government agencies in this city sending telegrams for accounting purposes have also been sent out by this Bureau. Telegrams will be accepted based on the printed telegram paper and this book starting July 1st. If there are any omissions or non-deliveries, please send a letter to this Bureau for inquiry.

Issuance of Multiple-Ride Tickets

The Traffic Department of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, for the convenience of passengers traveling to and from Shanghai, will issue multiple-ride tickets on its branch lines starting July 1st of this year. The notice and summary of regulations for issuance are listed below: Notice is hereby given that, for the convenience of passengers, the Shanghai branch line of this railway will temporarily pilot the issuance of two types of multiple-ride tickets, ten-ride and twenty-ride, starting July 1st. The ten-ride ticket will be charged at 85% of the regular fare and will be valid for two months. The twenty-ride ticket will be charged at 70% of the regular fare and will be valid for four months. A summary of the rules is on the left: 1. When boarding, the ticket must be submitted to the ticket office at the departure station for stamping with the date and train number; otherwise, boarding will not be permitted. If traveling with a ticket that has not been stamped, a supplementary ticket must be purchased. 2. The ticket will be inspected by the ticket inspector in accordance with regulations, and the stub will be sequentially collected by the ticket collector at the arrival station. Passengers must tear off the stub themselves. Torn-off tickets are invalid. 3. If disembarking mid-journey, a stub must still be collected. 4. If the ticket is used for travel beyond the station, a supplementary fare will be charged in accordance with regulations. 5. Once the ticket has been issued, it will not be refunded or exchanged. 6. If the ticket is lost, it will not be reissued. 7. This ticket is limited to personal use only. 8. All railway regulations apply, except for those specifically provided for in the issuance rules.

Architectural Association Sends Personnel to Beiping for Investigation; Expected Return Next Month; This Trip Has Gathered Abundant Materials

The Shanghai Architectural Association, in view of the fact that domestic construction projects in recent years have favored Europeanization, with all building materials used by construction companies being imported, resulting in significant annual losses, has specially dispatched construction engineers Du Yengeng, Liu Jiasheng, Du Junran, etc., to Beiping to investigate the construction of the Forbidden City, in order to incorporate Western designs upon their return and transform them into economical and sturdy new-style buildings. Extremely Hot Weather; Both Courts Change Office Hours; Office Closed in the Afternoon

Shen Jiayi, President of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court, and Wang Zhennan, Chief Prosecutor of the Court, in view of the summer season and the increasingly hot weather, will, in accordance with the usual practice, revise the office hours during the week. From July 1st to August 31st, work will begin at 8:00 a.m. every day, and rest will be taken at 1:00 p.m. The office will remain closed all day on Sundays. A notice has already been jointly issued yesterday to inform the public. The First Special District Local Court, which is located in the same place as the Second Branch of the Higher Court, will also have the same working hours during the summer vacation as the Second Branch of the Higher Court. Therefore, in the next two months, the Higher and Local Courts of the First Special District in this city will generally not hear ordinary civil and criminal cases in the afternoon, except for urgent cases that require immediate handling. However, the court opening time in the morning will be advanced by one hour.

Minutes of the South District Rent Reduction Association Meeting

The Shanghai South District Rent Reduction Association held a meeting yesterday at Yongqing Lane, Minquan Road. Shao Tinglu, Wang Xiekun, Tao Xianghua, Chen Wenju, Ni Yi, etc., were present, with Shen Xinfu elected as chairman and Ni Yi as recorder. The following resolutions were passed: 1. Regarding the case of the entire city of Shanghai unanimously refusing to reduce rent and pay rent, with requests for rent reduction coming from various lanes, which are being answered one by one but there are concerns about whether they can be fulfilled, and fears of lawsuits if landlords use this as an excuse, it was resolved that those requesting rent reduction must come to the association and explain the reasons for the reduction in detail. After the association sends a letter to the landlord, the rent must be deposited in the bank for legal resolution. 2. Regarding the case of landlords filing lawsuits in court on the grounds of rent arrears, it was resolved to send a letter to the Real Estate Association, forwarding it to its members, stating that if the Rent Reduction Association has sent a letter stating the reasons for the reduction and the rent has been deposited in the bank before the consultation is resolved, please do not arbitrarily initiate lawsuits. If the society is unsettled as a result, those who initiated the lawsuits shall bear full responsibility. 3. Regarding the case of publishing publications based on Article 11, Clause 5 of the association's charter, in addition to submitting them to the political party organs for registration, and requesting the assistance of famous writers from Shanghai for editing, what should be done about businesses and manufacturers of national goods posting advertisements? It was resolved that all businesses and households related to rent reduction must receive the publications. Advertisements for purely national goods will not be charged. The deadline for submissions is July 3rd. 4. Regarding the case of people using the name of rent reduction but neither paying rent nor depositing rent in the bank, it was resolved that the association cannot provide protection as they have not registered with the association. 5. Regarding the case that rent reductions have already been implemented in the capital and Anqing, but have not yet become widespread in Shanghai, it was resolved that the Municipal Government has sent a letter to the Council requesting a consultation, and the association has sent personnel to attend. Most of those registered with the association requesting rent reduction have already been resolved. The association will not intervene where there is no indication that rent is high. 6. Regarding the case of petitioning the Ministry of Justice to protect the residence of Shanghai citizens and curb rent disputes, it was resolved that the Secretariat should draft the petition and issue it within three days. The meeting adjourned after the resolutions were passed.

Yangtze Flour Mill Adopts Domestic Machinery

The Xie Da Machinery Factory, a member of the Shanghai Copper and Iron Machinery Industry Association, located at 314 Kunming Road, manufactures flour milling machinery and sells it throughout the country for many years. The factory has been carefully researching and has made many improvements in manufacturing in recent years. The original machinery of the Nanjing Yangtze Flour Company was purchased from abroad. Recently, due to the expansion of its business, the output was insufficient to meet demand. In order to promote domestic machinery, it specially purchased new machinery from Xie Da Machinery Factory. Since it was put into trial use, the results have been very excellent. Compared with the original foreign machinery, it can be on par, and the value is even cheaper. From now on, flour mills in our country can purchase domestic machinery to avoid outflowing of profits to foreign countries. It is heard that the Yangtze Company has given Xie Da Machinery Factory much encouragement and is introducing it, which is also good news in the promotion of domestic machinery.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sends Letter to French Municipal Council to Issue Certificates for Lost Vehicle Permits

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the French Concession Municipal Council yesterday, stating: "Respectfully, on the 28th of this month, according to a letter from the Rickshaw Industry Association, the members of the Association pay donations and obtain licenses from the French Concession Municipal Council every month, with each person's donation amount specified and reliable shop guarantees on file. However, when vehicles are operating outside, licenses are often lost or stolen due to the rickshaw pullers' carelessness or other reasons. Once lost, it is necessary to wait until the new license is received after the next month's donation before business can resume. During the period after the license is lost and before the new license is received, it is impossible to operate within the French Concession, resulting in considerable losses. The Association previously sent a letter to the French Municipal Council requesting that, in accordance with the regulations of the Municipal Finance Bureau, when a French license is lost or stolen, the Association should issue a letter of proof, and a temporary permit should be issued to allow continued business. We respectfully request that your Council appeal on behalf of the Association and earnestly request the French Municipal Council to promptly implement the aforementioned method for the sake of business, which is truly a matter of public convenience." After investigating, it was found that the license is lost, it will be required to pay the donation for the next month before they are renewed, and the time between the lost time and the renewed time is long, the loss of the rickshaw is definitely not small. Our municipal finance bureau already has the method of supplying temporary permit when the license is lost, then your board do the same thing in Shanghai area, it will be very convenient, and the benefit of rickshaw business is great. Accordingly, we send you the letter, please follow suit, it is real a public affair."

Zhang Asi, a Bandit, Found to Be Related to the Assassination of Du Nanxi

Du Nanxi, a native of Sichuan, 23 years old, graduated from the Municipal Administration Department of Fudan University and returned to Sichuan after becoming engaged to Ding Suhui, a female classmate from Jinshan. In March of last year, Du came to Shanghai from Sichuan to get married. Because Ms. Ding returned to Jinshan at this time, Du stayed at the Fudan University dormitory in Jiangwan. On the morning of the 24th of the same month, he came to Shanghai alone. At around 8:00 a.m., he was assassinated in front of No. 48, Puqing Lane, Malan Road, in the French Concession. The French Police reported the body to the Second Special District Court for identification. The deceased's cousin, Zhong Bojie, claimed the body and took it away for burial. After the case occurred, the French Police ordered Chinese and foreign detectives to investigate and arrest the murderer, but it has not been solved to this day. Zhang Asi, a 24-year-old bandit from Suzhou, was arrested last year in the Public Concession for committing gang robbery and possessing firearms. After being interrogated by the First Special District Court, he was sentenced to 15 years of imprisonment on April 28th of the same year and sent to the Tilanqiao Prison to serve his sentence. Recently, Zhang confessed in prison that he was also related to the shooting of Du Nanxi. Therefore, the Warden notified the Police, who informed the French Police. The Second Special District Court was requested to prepare a document, and Jin Jiulin, the Inspector General of the Special Agency, dispatched detectives Cai Jinzhang and Zuo Qihong to the First Special District Court the day before yesterday to transfer Zhang Asi to the case. Yesterday, he was escorted to the Second Special District Local Court, where Judge Wang Gangxu of the Criminal Division presided over the trial in the Criminal Court. Gu Shuxi, the Police lawyer, stated the case and requested a postponement of the investigation and then a trial. Zhang Asi confessed that the matter was done by Xiao Wang, who is at large. Before the incident, Xiao Wang borrowed a handgun from me, saying he wanted to kill an enemy. I lent him the handgun. When the incident happened, I also went along and stood at the entrance of the alley, waiting for the matter to be completed, so that I could ask Xiao Wang to return the handgun, to prevent him from discarding it after the incident. Afterwards, at the Xin Xin Hotel, Xiao Wang told me that he, Shi Guisheng, who is at large, and the deceased were selling opium together, which they brought from Sichuan to Shanghai to sell, but it was all embezzled by the deceased, so he wanted to kill him out of anger. He also said that the matter was very simple. I have fully explained the matter to the Police, and there is no need for further investigation. I request to be detained in the detention center during the period of the change for the trial. The court considered that the Police still need to investigate the case in detail and cannot change the detention to the detention center. It was ordered to postpone the trial to July 10th for further investigation. Zhang heard the order and asked the court that if the Police needed to investigate, he requested a shorter period, as he did not want to be detained in the Police Station. The judge then ordered that the period be shortened, and the trial was rescheduled to July 5th. After the order, the defendant was taken back to the Police Station for investigation by the detectives.

The Case of the "Fishing Ao Guest" Sent Back for Retrial

Wen Ying, the female disciple of the itinerant fortune-teller "Fishing Ao Guest" (named Cheng Meixian), was killed by her lover, Fan Hongsheng, a few years ago. The Police arrested Fan and sent him to the First Special District Local Court, where he was sentenced to imprisonment. After imprisonment, the deceased's mother, Wang Wu, claimed that her daughter was defiled by Cheng when she followed Cheng to study art, and that Fan's daring to attack with a weapon was also instigated by Cheng. Therefore, she filed a private prosecution against Cheng for interfering with the family. After the initial trial, Cheng was found not guilty. The woman refused to accept the verdict and specially made a vest with characters sewn on it, which she wore all year round, traveling back and forth between Beijing and Shanghai, appealing for justice everywhere. She also appealed to the Second Branch of the Higher Court, requesting that the original verdict be overturned and that Cheng be brought to justice. Subsequently, the first instance resulted in Cheng being found guilty and sentenced to one year of imprisonment. However, Cheng also refused to accept the verdict and appealed to the Supreme Court. After review, the Supreme Court found that the judgment of the second instance was not entirely appropriate. It has now been sent back to the Second Branch of the Higher Court for retrial, in order to prevent any miscarriage of justice and establish credibility. Yesterday morning, Judge Yu summoned both parties for examination. Since there are still witnesses who need to be summoned, he ordered a postponement for further investigation.

Fire at Kangqu Road Hat Factory Spreads to Six Neighboring Houses; Fire Starter Taken to District Bureau for Interrogation

The Zi Qiang Chemical Society at 357 Kangqu Road, Nanshi, specializes in bleaching straw hats for customers. The factory owner, Li Mianshi, from Wuxi, has been in business for some time, and the business is doing well. The factory has a total of eight rooms, surrounded by a bamboo fence. Yesterday at noon, around 12:00 p.m., during lunchtime, a fire suddenly broke out near the house. The bamboo fence burned in an instant, with loud explosions. The fire quickly spread to the kitchen. Residents nearby saw the fire and immediately reported it to Xing Yu, the police officer on duty at the Municipal Public Security Bureau, who immediately notified the fire brigades of each district and dispatched fire trucks to put out the fire. However, the fire had already become a raging blaze. Fortunately, the firefighters worked hard to extinguish the fire, and it was extinguished in about an hour. In addition to destroying three kitchens of the factory, it also spread to six neighboring houses. The scene was chaotic at the time. Wang Shouhe, the police chief of the Second District, led the police to maintain order and investigate the cause of the fire. Li Shanchu, a fire starter from Wuxi, was taken to the district bureau for interrogation.

Why Did Two Young Girls Commit Suicide? One Dead, One Also Not Saved

At 10:15 a.m. yesterday, two young girls, both around 17 or 18 years old, were found run over on the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway behind the Salt Depot in the jurisdiction of the Tanziwan Substation of the Fourth District Public Security Bureau, Zhabei. One was already dead, with a shattered skull, brain matter flowing out, and blood and flesh everywhere, a truly tragic sight. The deceased was wearing a short green "freedom cloth" shirt and black woolen pants, with a bob haircut, fashionable. The other girl also had her hair cut short, wore a short green "freedom cloth" shirt, red woolen pants, and was also injured in the head, but had not yet died. Inspector Jiang Dianle then dispatched police chief Lu Huaigong and others to investigate and confirmed the facts. He also reported to Gong Xikui, the District Chief of the Fourth District, instructing him to first report the incident to the Supervision Department of the Public Security Bureau by telephone and send the girl who had not yet died to the hospital. However, after examination by the doctor, it was found that the injured girl could not be saved. As neither of the two girls was claimed by their families at the time, Inspector Jiang immediately notified the Railway Police Department by telephone, instructing Zhang Fengqi, the local guarantor of the 23rd district of the department, to report the incident to the Shanghai Local Court for examination.

Yesterday, because he delayed the payment, the court, at the plaintiff's request, sent a bailiff to summon the defendant to the court to investigate. The court questioned Wang, but he was evasive. Grand Opening of Zheng Daihe's Solo Exhibition; Starting July 1st at the Old Youth Association

Zheng Daihe, a painter and calligrapher from Wujin, is well-versed in the national essence of painting and believes that calligraphy and painting are enough to cultivate the mind and enhance intelligence. In the past, he followed the famous painter Wu Guandai from Xishan for many years, researching deeply and gaining more and more achievements. He has long been renowned in the art world and praised in Suzhou and Changzhou. Zheng's landscapes capture the true essence of Wen, Shen, Tang, and Wang, while his figures trace back to Longmian and Liuru. His recent imitations of Ying Piaozi's works also reveal an ancient atmosphere. In particular, his birds, flowers, insects, and scales can move freely between Xinluo and Baiyang. With a wave of his hand, he captures the natural charm and is truly a masterpiece. In the past few years, he has held solo exhibitions in Su, Xi, Jing, Han, and even Wuhu and Changsha, which have been highly praised by celebrities and gentry in various places. This time, he did not hesitate to come to Shanghai in the heat, bringing more than 200 of his carefully crafted masterpieces from the past ten years to hold an exhibition at the Shi Bao Guan, promoting art and elucidating the national essence. His ambitions are commendable. The details have been recorded in this newspaper in the past. Yesterday was the second day of Zheng's painting exhibition. Although it was under the scorching sun, with the Fahrenheit thermometer rising to over 100 degrees, people from all walks of life and lovers of calligraphy and painting still braved the heat to visit. In recent days, the number of guests attending the exhibition has been no less than several hundred thousand. Everyone praised Zheng's works, saying that his accomplishments are profound and different from ordinary people. They lingered and were reluctant to leave. In particular, the tiger painting was miraculously rendered. The old pine and strange rocks are also vigorous and beautiful, taking the ancient method, with green and blue landscapes, breathing in the spirit of the Song people, and closely following the mountains and valleys, Wang Xizhi's fan, snow-covered bamboo, returning herds at sunset, pine forest longevity Buddha, Magu offering wine, and birds and flowers, all have their own unique features. In particular, the Shudao Hanyun Tu handscroll, imitating Wang Qingqing's original, is as long as three zhang, and is even more precious with the inscriptions of famous calligraphers and painters such as Hu Tinglu, Zhang Shijun, Wu Jingyu, Qian Zhenhuang, Yan Ganyuan, Deng Chunshu, Yu Baoqing, and Tang Danran. Zheng's painting exhibition is scheduled to be held at the Sichuan Road Youth Association from July 1st to 3rd. It is easier for visiting guests to travel back and forth. At the same time, July 1st to 3rd is the annual holiday for the Shanghai banking industry. It is expected that those who go to the Sichuan Road Youth Association to visit will be even more crowded.

This is truly a must-read for every pregnant woman. It is said that in order to make the majority of pregnant families generally understand safe childbirth methods, Dr. Guo has reprinted this book for wide distribution. Those who wish to obtain this book can send a letter with postage stamps (2 cents for local areas, 8 cents for outside areas) to the Guo Taihua Gynecology Hospital on Maithes Road and it will be mailed immediately.

▲Dr. Tu Qihua's book "A Brief Discussion on Venereal Diseases": Dr. Tu Qihua has been in Shanghai County for more than ten years. He specializes in venereal dermatology and reproductive urology to relieve the suffering of people in society and has gained the trust of the community. The wife of Mr. Wang Dasheng of Hefeng Rice Store on Huanghe Road suffered from stubborn tinea for many years and sought treatment from famous Chinese and Western doctors, but without any improvement. After Dr. Tu's diagnosis and treatment, she was completely cured in less than two weeks. Reservations are now being accepted and will receive preferential treatment, only charging 30 cents for the cost.

▲Administering a Prescription is Better than Administering Medicine: Mr. Wu Shuhe, an expert in internal medicine, can be said to spare no effort in popularizing medical knowledge. Reading Q&A: Mei Lanfang and the Future of Chinese Old Opera | Reply to Mr. Li Ruhui | Reading Guidance:

After reading Mr. Shiheng's "Mei Lanfang's Performance in Russia" on the Torch of the 17th Dagong Daily, I can't help but have the following questions:

1. The artistic value of Chinese old opera: In the article, Mr. Shiheng first cited the three reasons why Mr. Jizi opposes old opera (the original text has not been read): 1. The gongs and drums in Peking opera are not music; 2. Cross-dressing belongs to the art of primitive drama and is vulgar and unbearable; 3. Men singing female voices or women singing male voices are unnatural and somewhat comical. Then, he further completely denied the artistic value of old opera, believing that "old opera is an art of a barbaric society, and in any case, it cannot be suitable for modern society." Therefore, he said, "I ask, which person who understands art can tolerate the noise of gongs and drums, the strange laughter and crying?" And then, "Which person who appreciates art can see the red-bearded painted faces, the strange costumes that cannot exist in any era?" Is Chinese old opera really as Mr. Shiheng said, without any artistic value? I don't quite believe it! Not to mention anything else, just its long history and widespread circulation do not allow us to deny it uncritically. The existence of a thing must have its social basis and its own value for existence. I am not a "national essence school" intentionally speaking up for old opera, but I feel that Mr. Shiheng's obliteration of everything cannot convince people, and only exposes his own lack of understanding of drama. For example, opposing classical Chinese cannot deny the artistry of all classical Chinese. Can we say that Lisao, the Book of Songs, and the poems of Li Du have no artistry? Moreover, what standards is Mr. Shiheng using for his so-called "artistic"? This is the first thing I ask you to answer.

2. Why does the Soviet Union want to invite Mei Lanfang? Regarding the reasons why the Soviet Union wants to invite Mei Lanfang to perform, two points can be seen from the article. One is what the reporter who reported this news quoted, saying that "the whole world has recognized that Chinese drama is full of symbolism, and the Soviet Russian art world is also popularizing symbolism, so they want to appreciate Dr. Mei's art." The other is what Mr. Shiheng himself said, that "Soviet Russia has the spare money to invite Mr. Mei to perform" and "for the sake of novelty." I dare not believe either of these statements: Mr. Shiheng also briefly explained whether Chinese drama is symbolism, but what about the Soviet Union? According to what I have heard, socialist realism is popular, and realism has not only not declined but has also been elevated to a new stage. Why is symbolism popular again? I think it is a pity that Mr. Shiheng did not specifically explain this. As for what Mr. Shiheng said, it is even closer to joking. Even if the Soviet Union has spare money, and even though the Soviet Union spares no effort in cultural construction, it will never blindly and curiously invite Mei Lanfang to "sightsee"? However, what is the reason why the Soviet Union invited Mei Lanfang to perform? This is the second thing I ask you to answer.

3. The future of Chinese drama: Although the Chinese spoken drama movement has made considerable progress, to be fair, old opera still occupies a very large position in the minds of the public. Not only in rural areas is it completely the power of old opera, but even in large cities, spoken drama and film are only opposed to old opera. Of course, as a whole, old opera should be resolutely opposed, and the decline of old opera is inevitable. However, drama is the most popular art. If we want to create more popular drama, we cannot but pay attention to the subjective and objective conditions that enable old opera to attract a large audience. May I ask, when we are vehemently opposing old opera and building new drama, and when we are deciding on the future of the drama movement, is this not a question that should be specifically raised? This is the third thing I ask you to answer.

The above three points are not only my personal questions, I think they must also be the questions of many drama lovers. I hope you will give us a correct answer as soon as possible. Li Ruhui

Joint Graduation Ceremony of Elementary Schools in This City ▲ Speeches by Guests Dong Renjian, etc. ▲ Arithmetic Repêchage Awards Given at the Same Time

A notice was specially issued yesterday as follows:

Notice from the Municipal Education Bureau, Shanghai Education Bureau, stating, "Case received: Instruction No. 4270 from the Ministry of Education states, 'A review of the statistics on the results of the student examinations in secondary schools in the 21st year shows that subjects such as mathematics, physics, chemistry, and biology are the worst. The reason may be that the teaching materials are not suitable or the teaching methods are not good. Teachers must first strive to enrich and improve the content and methods of the subjects they are teaching in order to improve the students' level. This work should be carried out by the schools, using all conveniences, to seek remedy according to their needs. The bureaus are instructed to directly consult with the designated nearby universities to handle this matter, or to carefully plan and handle it at other appropriate schools. Mathematics, 2. Biology, 3. Physics, 4. Chemistry. ㈢ Training Content: The training content focuses on: 1. New developments in each subject (approximately 25%), 2. Research on teaching methods and teaching materials (approximately 50%), 3. Research on experiments and equipment (approximately 25%). ㈣ Admission Qualifications: All current science teachers in public and private registered secondary schools in this city, except for those who have good qualifications and are specially allowed to be exempt from attending lectures, should register for admission by determining the subjects they wish to study. Science teachers who are currently teaching in unregistered secondary schools in this city, and those who will be or wish to be science teachers in public and private secondary schools in this city, and whose qualifications are still in line with those of secondary school teachers, should also register first, and may be allowed to attend lectures when there are vacancies. ㈤ Enrollment: The total number of people in each group is limited to 300. ㈥ Lecturers: Professors with specialized knowledge in each subject and rich experience from public and private universities in this city will be hired as lecturers. ㈦ Duration: From July 12th (Monday) to August 15th (Wednesday). ㈧ Registration and Admission: All applicants for registration must fill out two registration forms and pay the fees in accordance with the regulations. ㈨ Registration Dates: From July 9th (Monday) to July 14th (Saturday). ㈩ Lecture Time: Except for Sundays, the class time is from 7:30 AM to 9:30 AM every day, and the discussion or experiment time is from 3:30 PM to 5:30 PM. ㈩㈠ Fees: All registered students should pay a tuition fee of 10 yuan, an experiment fee of 5 yuan, a lecture note fee of 2 yuan, and a accommodation fee of 2 yuan. Statistics on Students Studying Abroad in the Past Three Years

A Total of 2,317 People

▲ From the 19th Year to the 22nd Year

▲ Results of a Survey by the World Chinese Students' Federation

The World Chinese Students' Federation has been organizing study abroad receptions for more than 20 years. In addition to providing services, it also emphasizes survey and statistical work. Recently, the association compiled statistics on students studying abroad in the past three years from the 19th year, the 20th year, and the 21st year. From July of the 19th year to June of the 22nd year, there were a total of 2,317 people from our country studying abroad.

▲ Country Comparison: The largest number of students studied in Japan, accounting for one-third of the total, with 1,031 people. The United States, France, Germany, England, Belgium, Austria, and other countries followed. Canada, Italy, the Philippines, Sweden, India, Denmark, Poland, the Netherlands, and other countries had fewer. If compared by the

▲ Year of Departure: The 19th year had the most, with 1,229 people. The 21st year was second, with 547 people. The 20th year had the fewest, with only 541 people. If compared by the

▲ Province of Origin of the Students: Guangdong Province had the most, followed by Zhejiang, Jiangsu, Liaoning, Fujian, Hubei, Hebei, Hunan, Sichuan, Anhui, Shandong, Jiangxi, Henan, Yunnan, Shaanxi, and other provinces. Xinjiang and Jehol provinces had the fewest. If compared by the students'

▲ School of Origin: Peiping University had the most, with 66 people. Peking University, Yenching, Central, Fudan, Chaoyang, Peiping Normal University, Zhonggong, Jinling, Tongji, Southeast University, Jiaotong, Hujiang, Jinan, Zhongshan, and other universities were slightly less. The Central Political School, Central Military Academy, Chengdu University, Daxia University, and various middle schools had fewer, averaging only three or four people. According to the association's reporter in Shanghai, the number of people studying abroad after the 19th year has decreased significantly compared to before the 19th year. The reason is the impact of high gold prices and unstable political situations. It is also said that this record of students studying abroad has now been published and will be available to the public soon for reference. The price is particularly affordable.
